---
title: Awakener Guides
description: Quick reference character guides covering roles, DPS and support rankings, optimal team setups, and builds for new players, including key power spike enlightens and recommended gear.
icon: lucide/book-user
---

<figure markdown="span">
  ![](/images/emojis/doll-peeking.png){width="196"}
</figure>

# Awakener Guides

<div class="accordion no-icon" markdown>
??? quote "About the Awakener Guides"

    These quick reference guides summarize what each character does and how they're normally used by veteran players. They also suggest wheels, covenants, posses, and teammates that each character can use.

    Each character's DPS Rank and Support Rank refers to that character's rank in the [Tier List (For New Players)](/handbook/tier-list), where you can find a description of what each rank means.

    "Stopping Points" refers to specific enlightens (dupes) where the character has a power spike. If it says "E0" or "Any," it means the character is worth using even without any enlightens. Otherwise, it means the character is significantly weaker without at least the listed enlightens.

    **The suggested builds are "poverty newbie builds."** They assume you're doing normal story or low alert D-Effect Zone and don't have many wheels other than those in the [SSR Wheel Tier List](/handbook/wheels). For endgame builds with all limited wheels and +12 wheels, you can consult other resources such as in-game leaderboards or the [Mythag Compendium](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1TCU7LJRzqKeuvLe97y_TfGZ-j6jq5bZX6hskAAJ2mFQ/){target="_blank"}.

??? quote "Contents"

    **[Chaos:](#chaos)** ["24"](#24) [Alva](#alva) [Doll](#doll) [GDoll](#gdoll) [Hameln](#hameln) [Kathigu-Ra](#kathigu-ra) [Karen](#karen) [Lily](#lily) [Lotan](#lotan) [Mouchette](#mouchette) [Nautila](#nautila) [Nymphaea](#nymphaea) [Ogier](#ogier) [Pandia](#pandia) [Ramona](#ramona) [GRamona](#gramona) [Ryker](#ryker) [Tawil](#tawil)

    **[Aequor:](#aequor)** [Aurita](#aurita) [Caecus](#caecus) [Celeste](#celeste) [Corposant](#corposant) [Faros](#faros) [Goliath](#goliath) [Miryam](#miryam) [Murphy](#murphy) [Sanga](#sanga) [Tulu](#tulu) <br /> **[Divine Realm: Aequor:](#divine-realm-aequor)** [GMurphy](#gmurphy) [Vortice](#vortice)

    **[Caro:](#caro)** [Agrippa](#agrippa) [Aigis](#aigis) [Doresain](#doresain) [Faint](#faint) [Helot](#helot) [GHelot](#ghelot) [Leigh](#leigh) [Pickman](#pickman) [Salvador](#salvador) [Sorel](#sorel) [Thais](#thais) [Uvhash](#uvhash) [Xu](#xu) <br /> **[Propagation: Caro:](#propagation-caro)** [Saya](#saya)

    **[Ultra:](#ultra)** [Casiah](#casiah) [Castor](#castor) [Clementine](#clementine) [Daffodil](#daffodil) [Erica](#erica) [Horla](#horla) [Jenkin](#jenkin) [Liz](#liz) [Pollux](#pollux) [Tinct](#tinct) [Wanda](#wanda) [Winkle](#winkle) <br /> **[Singularity: Ultra:](#singularity-ultra)** [Arachne](#arachne)
</div>

## Chaos

### "24" {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Exalt Spamming DPS & Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Keyflare &middot;
    Poison &middot;
    Embryo &middot;
    Counter &middot;
    Aliemus &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span>
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["24"](/images/awakeners/chaos/24.png "&quot;24&quot;"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E2, E3</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A flexible, high-damage support whose abilities vary according to the realm she's used with.</p>

Chaos "24" deals enough single-target damage that she's a viable endgame DPS against bosses. Ultra "24" is also very strong in [Faded Legacy](/handbook/storylines#faded-legacy-arc-1), but got nerfed into the ground in [Astral Reign](/handbook/storylines#astral-reign-arc-2).</p>

"24" likes teammates who can grant aliemus to fuel her exalt spam, or who synergize with poison (in Aequor) or counter (in Ultra).</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Alva {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Anti-Bullshit Support / Shield Strike Combo DPS
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Dispel Seal &middot;
    Discard Symptoms &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    Alert &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    Strikes
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Alva"](/images/awakeners/chaos/alva.png "Alva"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">*Support:* Any · *DPS:* E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Some of the hardest stages fill your hand with crap and seal you so you can't do anything. Alva counters them by getting rid of seals and symptoms, while providing shields and vulnerable with her exalt.

At E3, she can be a DPS that sets up burst combos with Combat Stance and Precision Slash. This works best if her team makes lots of shields and can copy or replay her cards.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Doll {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Cheap Defensive Keyflare Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    Aliemus &middot;
    Heals &middot;
    Discard &middot;
    Dispel Vulnerable
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Doll"](/images/awakeners/chaos/doll.png "Doll"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">F *(???)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E1, E3</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Doll is the best weakness applier among all standard characters — great for surviving harder difficulties on a new account.

Equivalent Exchange can discard symptoms and status cards inflicted by enemies, useful for overcoming mechanics in specific fights.

She also generates a bit of healing and aliemus, and her high base Keyflare Regen makes her a good [keyflare bot](/handbook/team#the-almighty-keyflare-bot).
</div>
</div>
</div>

### GDoll {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Boss-Destroying Aliemus Battery
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Aliemus &middot;
    DMG Amp. &middot;
    HP % Damage &middot;
    Poison &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    Heals
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["GDoll"](/images/awakeners/chaos/gdoll.png "GDoll"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>
    
    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *against bosses*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E1, E2, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A versatile aliemus battery who brings big [DMG amplification](/handbook/team#dmg-amplification-base-dmg) buffs and access to both weakness and vulnerable at E1. She shines in poison teams, but works as an aliemus support anywhere.

Her true strength is in boss fights, where she deletes 25-30% of a boss's HP bar and gives your team a massive boost in Finale Form.

At OE, she can carry boss fights by herself.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Hameln {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Arithmetica Printer & Card Copyist
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Arith. &middot;
    Card Draw &middot;
    Card Copy &middot;
    STR Steal &middot;
    Multihit &middot;
    Pierce DMG
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Hameln"](/images/awakeners/chaos/hameln.png "Hameln"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E2</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A utility support who draws cards, copies card effects, and gives you 2 extra arithmetica every turn when roused.

He can set up near-infinite combo turns in [Faded Legacy](/handbook/storylines#faded-legacy-arc-1), but falls off in [Astral Reign](/handbook/storylines#astral-reign-arc-2) because of the soft cap on cards played per turn.

Works best with teammates that want to combo off and play a lot of cards.
</div>
</div>
</div>

</section>

### Kathigu-Ra {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Tanky Ramping Juggernaut
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    AOE &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    STR &middot;
    Pierce DMG
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Kathigu-Ra"](/images/awakeners/chaos/kathigu-ra.png "Kathigu-Ra"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A bruiser who can generate huge shields with her defense card in addition to huge damage.

Her damage starts low, but she rapidly gains Base DMG and STR by playing cards with Fiamma and resetting with 0-cost Hyperflares. After ramping, Hyperflare can one-shot bosses.

Kath needs E3 and her posse to work. She likes teammates who provide STR and crit buffs, as well as arithmetica to fuel her Combust cycles.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>

  [![Tinct](/images/awakeners/ultra/tinct--mini.png "Tinct"){loading=lazy}](#tinct) <figcaption>[Tinct](#tinct)</figcaption>
  </figure>
  <figure markdown="span">
  [![Karen](/images/awakeners/chaos/karen--mini.png "Karen"){loading=lazy}](#karen) <figcaption>[Karen](#karen)</figcaption>
  </figure>
</div>
</section>

### Karen {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Arithmetica Delivery Service
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Arith. &middot;
    Poison &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    Heals &middot;
    Dispel Stagnation
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Karen"](/images/awakeners/chaos/karen.png "Karen"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">Any, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Karen's exalt banks 3 arithmetica you can use at any time (and applies random buffs at E3). This makes her a cheap but effective support for characters that need a lot of arithmetica. She applies decent poison in [Astral Reign](/handbook/storylines#astral-reign-arc-2) too.

While her skills are weak, they can be retained for defensive utility at the right moment, or simply held so they don't go back into the deck.

OE makes her a top-tier arithmetica support.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Lily {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Immortal Poison Tank
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Shields &middot;
    Heals &middot;
    Poison &middot;
    Strikes
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Lily"](/images/awakeners/chaos/lily.png "Lily"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
One of the best defensive awakeners. When invested and loaded up with death resistance stats, an E3 Lily can outheal all incoming damage and carry the entire team.

She deals a surprising amount of damage as well, making her a strong secondary DPS.

Lily works best as the main shielder and healer in poison teams, but she can fit in any team that has trouble surviving.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Lotan {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Strike-Spamming Exalt DPS
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Strikes &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Multihit &middot;
    HP % Damage
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Lotan"](/images/awakeners/chaos/lotan.png "Lotan"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *at OE*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A damage dealer who uses 0-cost Blade of Defiance combos to power up her exalt. While she's decent at clearing mobs, she struggles with sustained damage on bosses with a lot of HP.

Her Over-Exalt deals bonus damage equal to 15% of the enemy's max HP. This boosts her damage a lot and makes her worth bringing as a support purely for her OE.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Mouchette {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Death-Defying Glass Cannon DPS
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Multihit &middot;
    Strikes &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Death Res. Abuse &middot;
    Stun
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Mouchette"](/images/awakeners/chaos/mouchette.png "Mouchette"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-s);">S *(Insane)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">F *(???)*</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *at OE*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E2, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
One of the highest-damage carries in the game. Even the toughest endgame bosses tremble in fear when they hear "Shining ✰ Tornaaaaado!" In normal story mode she melts everything with her exalt and Mortal Blast combos.

Needs E3 for her full damage potential. She works best on a team loaded up with death resistance, as her E1 gives stacking buffs each time you trigger death resistance in the fight.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build</div>

### Nautila {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Shield Stall & Counter Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Shields &middot;
    Aliemus &middot;
    Temp. Counter &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Debuff Immunity
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Nautila"](/images/awakeners/chaos/nautila.png "Nautila"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E2, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A solid defensive support and combo piece. Her unique exalt takes your existing shield and multiplies it, which is amazing for shield scaling teammates like [Sanga](#sanga) and [Alva](#alva).

Nautila's exalt can support counter teams by converting counter into AOE damage. At E3, it also blocks incoming debuffs, useful for many boss fights.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Nymphaea {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Poison Trigger Keyflare Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Poison &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span>
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Nymphaea"](/images/awakeners/chaos/nymphaea.png "Nymphaea"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">*Support:* Any · *DPS:* E3, OE, +12</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Nymphaea's exalt instantly triggers poison, speeding up the long time poison teams usually take to kill enemies. She also boosts teamwide poison in [Astral Reign](/handbook/storylines#astral-reign-arc-2) stages, and her high base keyflare regen makes her a solid [keyflare bot](/handbook/team#the-almighty-keyflare-bot).

Works best in a team full of poison characters. Nymphaea's rouse makes her a decent poison applier, but she takes ages to ramp up, making her impractical as a DPS outside of boss fights.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Ogier {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Defensive STR Buffer
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Shields &middot;
    Temp. STR &middot;
    STR &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    Dispel Fragile
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Ogier"](/images/awakeners/chaos/ogier.png "Ogier"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">F *(???)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">OE, +12</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A shielder who gives a burst of temporary STR with his exalt, making him a good teammate for characters that rely on STR to deal damage.

Ogier scales well with investment and becomes crazy good at +12 and level 90 with +12 wheels. Before that, he is unfortunately outclassed by many other characters.
</div>
</div>
</div>

  </figure>

  [![Jenkin](/images/awakeners/ultra/jenkin--mini.png "Jenkin"){loading=lazy}](#jenkin) <figcaption>[Jenkin](#jenkin)</figcaption>
  </figure>
  <figure markdown="span">
  [![Liz](/images/awakeners/ultra/liz--mini.png "Liz"){loading=lazy}](#liz) <figcaption>[Liz](#liz)</figcaption>
  </figure>
  <figure markdown="span">
  [![Tawil](/images/awakeners/chaos/tawil--mini.png "Tawil"){loading=lazy}](#tawil) <figcaption>[Tawil](#tawil)</figcaption>
  </figure>
</div>
</section>

### Pandia {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Counter Removal Bot / Early Game Counter DPS
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Remove Enemy Counter &middot;
    Counter &middot;
    AOE
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Pandia"](/images/awakeners/chaos/pandia.png "Pandia"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c-plus);">C+ *(Niche)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">*Support:* Any · *DPS:* E1, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A niche support who is mainly used to remove counter from enemies with Wax-Hot Desire.

Pandia can be a main DPS at low levels. In [Faded Legacy](/handbook/storylines#faded-legacy-arc-1) stages, her exalt can convert counter into high damage.

She was caught in the crossfire when [Astral Reign](/handbook/storylines#astral-reign-arc-2) rules nerfed Ultra ["24"](#24), making her sadly unusable as a DPS for most endgame content.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Ramona {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Card Searching Keyflare Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Keyflare &middot;
    Card Draw &middot;
    Arith. Discount
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Ramona"](/images/awakeners/chaos/ramona.png "Ramona"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">Any, OE (You get her for free)</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A solid if unremarkable keyflare support. Her exalt is the main reason to use her over other supports: searching for any card and reducing its cost to 0 is very flexible and powerful.

She works best with teammates that have high-cost cards or specific cards they need.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### GRamona {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Time-Looping Toolbox
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Card Draw &middot;
    Posse Switch &middot;
    Keyflare
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["GRamona"](/images/awakeners/chaos/gramona.png "GRamona"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E2, E3, OE (You get her for free)</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A complex and versatile support. Her exalt gives you the last 3 cards you played last turn, which enables perfect setups for specific DPS she pairs well with. At E3, she also lets you replace your posse with anything you want, for instance getting Voices In Your Head for vulnerable and weakness on demand.

Her DPS build revolves around using dual posse every turn to scale Predetermined Strike. This is slow and not recommended for new players.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build (Keyflare Support)</div>

  [![Hameln](/images/awakeners/chaos/hameln--mini.png "Hameln"){loading=lazy}](#hameln) <figcaption>[Hameln](#hameln)</figcaption>
  </figure>
</div>
</section>

### Ryker {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    High-Rolling Damage Buff Dispenser
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Card Draw &middot;
    Crit Rate &middot;
    Crit DMG &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    Keyflare &middot;
    AOE
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Ryker"](/images/awakeners/chaos/ryker.png "Ryker"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">Any</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
An offensive support who gives you money and permanent upgrades as you progress through the exploration. All these small buffs add up to a big damage boost for boss fights.

Ryker is also excellent at drawing cards and searching for cards, making him a good teammate for characters that rely on specific cards to function.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Tawil {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    All-in-One Utility Toolbox
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Keyflare &middot;
    Discover &middot;
    Card Draw &middot;
    STR Steal &middot;
    Multihit &middot;
    HP % Damage
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Tawil"](/images/awakeners/chaos/tawil.png "Tawil"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b-plus);">B+ *(Good Early)*</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *at OE*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E2, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A ridiculously versatile support who can use cards from any character in the team or realm. Their wings do all kinds of stuff too.

Can cosplay as a DPS by spamming Four Wings to stack temporary STR, ending with Six Wings or other high-scaling cards. For new players, this is easiest with an Aequor team.

Needs E2 and lots of arithmetica to work well. Also very complex and time-consuming to play.
</div>
</div>
</div>

## Aequor

### Aurita {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Multihit Tentacle Driver
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Multihit &middot;
    Discard &middot;
    Card Draw &middot;
    Pierce DMG
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Aurita"](/images/awakeners/aequor/aurita.png "Aurita"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E1, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Aurita's gimmick is that she hits lots of times, triggering 25+ tentacle attacks in one turn when in Raging Waves stance. This makes her a good character for converting STR and Tentacle DMG into burst damage.

Her actual damage is low, so she needs a team that stacks lots of STR and Tentacle DMG, or another payoff for tentacle attacks such as [Faros](#faros) 's Deep Currents.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Caecus {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Offensive Healer / Counter Driver
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Heals &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    Counter &middot;
    Dispel Weakness
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Caecus"](/images/awakeners/aequor/caecus.png "Caecus"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E2</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A support with good healing over time and consistent access to vulnerable from his exalt. He can multiply counter triggers for one turn, making him a niche but strong counter support.

In fights where you can stall and build counter, Caecus works as a main DPS. His counter scales with STR and critical hits, making him one of the rare endgame viable counter stackers (with enough buffs from his teammates).
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Celeste {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Extra Life and Arithmetica Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Revive &middot;
    Arith. &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    Heals &middot;
    Dispel Blighten/Stagnation
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Celeste"](/images/awakeners/aequor/celeste.png "Celeste"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">F *(???)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">Any</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Celeste's unique exalt revives you from death once per fight (once every 6 turns at E3). This means that if you have a glass cannon DPS in danger of dying to normal mob fights, Celeste can carry your team all the way to the boss.

Celeste also generates a bit of arithmetica and Tentacle DMG, and her defensive skills can be retained so they don't clog your deck.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Corposant {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Discard-Abusing Story Mode Champion
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Discard &middot;
    Card Draw &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    STR &middot;
    Tentacle DMG &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span>
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Corposant"](/images/awakeners/aequor/corposant.png "Corposant"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b-plus);">B+ *(Good Early)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A flexible defensive and offensive support with access to both weakness and vulnerable at E3. In a discard-focused team that consistently triggers Aftershock, her Pilots rapidly stack STR and Tentacle DMG.

Corposant is notably strong in story mode and Hectic Skybound Rail, as she easily abuses many Ch. resonance gimmicks. Her [Astral Reign](/handbook/storylines#astral-reign-arc-2) soulforge talent makes her deal high damage to Aequor enemies, including Ch.-end bosses.
</div>
</div>
</div>

  </figure>
  <figure markdown="span">
  [![Casiah](/images/awakeners/ultra/casiah--mini.png "Casiah"){loading=lazy}](#casiah) <figcaption>[Casiah](#casiah)</figcaption>
  </figure>
  <figure markdown="span">
  [![Vortice](/images/awakeners/aequor/vortice--mini.png "Vortice"){loading=lazy}](#vortice) <figcaption>[Vortice](#vortice)</figcaption>
  </figure>
</div>
</section>

### Faros {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Defensive Card Draw Support / AOE Poison Applier
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Lemurian &middot;
    Card Draw &middot;
    Poison &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    Multihit &middot;
    Dispel Vulnerable
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Faros"](/images/awakeners/aequor/faros.png "Faros"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">*Support:* Any · *DPS:* E2, E3</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Faros's exalt is a powerful card selection tool which also provides a nice shield. Going into a fight with her exalt fully charged lets you start with a perfect opening hand, for example starting with all rouses in [Faded Legacy](/handbook/storylines#faded-legacy-arc-1) stages.

Faros can also be built as a DPS that spams Deep Currents to apply poison. This works best in a team full of poison units, or with a way to trigger a lot of tentacle attacks in one turn.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Goliath {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Lemurian STR Support / AOE Mob Clearer
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Lemurian &middot;
    Temp. STR &middot;
    STR &middot;
    STR Steal &middot;
    Strikes
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Goliath"](/images/awakeners/aequor/goliath.png "Goliath"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *( Usable)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E2</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
If you have tons of Tentacle DMG, Goliath's exalt makes tons of temporary STR with Usurp. This makes him the best offensive support for [Astral Reign](/handbook/storylines#astral-reign-arc-2) Lemurian teams with [Tulu](#tulu). His ability to steal STR is also useful in some fights.

Goliath is a solid DPS at low levels. His exalt cards and Decapitation Damage scale well with STR, making him good at cleaning up low-HP enemies even at endgame.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Miryam {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Versatile Ramping Aliemus Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Lemurian &middot;
    Aliemus &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    Heals &middot;
    Poison &middot;
    Crit DMG &middot;
    STR
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Miryam"](/images/awakeners/aequor/miryam.png "Miryam"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E2</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
The premier do-everything Aequor support. She makes aliemus, applies premium debuffs, boosts team damage, heals you when you're low, and even triggers poison for poison teams. Her only drawback is her reliance on her rouse.

At endgame, Miryam is usually seen supporting [GMurphy](#gmurphy) Lemurian teams, but she works great in any team comp that has blue in it.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build</div>
<div class="hagrid grid-1/1/1/1" markdown>

  </figure>
  <figure class="center" markdown="span">
    [![Burial Ground's Sighs](/images/covenants/burial-grounds-sighs.png "Burial Ground's Sighs"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#burial-grounds-sighs)
  </figure>
  <figure class="center" markdown="span">
    [![Deus Ex Machina](/images/covenants/deus-ex-machina--icon.png "Deus Ex Machina"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#deus-ex-machina)
  </figure>
  <figure class="center" markdown="span">
    [![Deus Ex Machina](/images/covenants/deus-ex-machina.png "Deus Ex Machina"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#deus-ex-machina)
  </figure>

### Murphy {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Damage-Delaying Keyflare Tank
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Delay Damage &middot;
    Keyflare &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    Arith.
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Murphy"](/images/awakeners/aequor/murphy.png "Murphy"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E1, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A keyflare support with great defense for any Aequor team that needs help surviving.

Her exalt converts incoming damage into damage over time, letting you survive massive attacks, then self-cleanse with Vortex Reversal.

Works well with [GMurphy](#gmurphy) even though she isn't a Lemurian, as she can clear [GMurphy](#gmurphy)'s self-inflicted sacrifice.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Sanga {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Mob Clearing Shield Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    AOE &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    Dispel Fragile
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Sanga"](/images/awakeners/aequor/sanga.png "Sanga"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *at OE*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E1, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
If you can stack a lot of shield in one turn, Sanga's exalt converts it into significant AOE damage. This makes her useful in stall teams that have trouble killing normal enemies fast.

Sanga can solo DPS at low levels, but she struggles with enemies that have a lot of HP. Unless you have her OE, or a support that multiplies her damage like [Saya](#saya), she's best used as a supportive secondary DPS.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Tulu {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    The King of Tentacle DMG
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Lemurian &middot;
    Temp. STR &middot;
    Tentacle DMG &middot;
    Crit Rate &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Dispel Weakness
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Tulu"](/images/awakeners/aequor/tulu.png "Tulu"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E1, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A support with one purpose: to make your tentacles hit like trucks. With the Tentacle DMG and crit rate from his exalt, other characters can deal high damage with multihit attacks in Raging Waves stance.

At low levels, Abyss Order and tentacle slaps are enough to make Tulu usable as a solo DPS. At endgame he is mainly used as a damage buffer in [Corposant](#corposant) or [GMurphy](#gmurphy) teams.
</div>
</div>
</div>

## Divine Realm: Aequor

### GMurphy {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Stance-Switching Keyflare Support-Carry
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Lemurian &middot;
    Card Draw &middot;
    Arith. &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    Sacrifice &middot;
    Multihit &middot;
    Tentacle DMG
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["GMurphy"](/images/awakeners/aequor/gmurphy.png "GMurphy"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b-plus);">B+ *(Good Early)*</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *at OE*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">*Support:* E0, E1, E3 · *DPS:* E2, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A high-damage support with amazing skills and powered-up tentacle stances — at a cost. Her stance cooldowns and self-inflicted damage force you to weigh her strong abilities against the price you have to pay later.

GMurphy is a viable endgame DPS with OE and high investment. In [Astral Reign](/handbook/storylines#astral-reign-arc-2) stages, she works well in all-Lemurian teams with [Miryam](#miryam), [Tulu](#tulu), [Goliath](#goliath), and/or [Faros](#faros).
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Vortice {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Ramping Artillery Cannon
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    AOE &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    Tentacle DMG &middot;
    Remove Fortress &middot;
    HP % Damage
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Vortice"](/images/awakeners/aequor/vortice.png "Vortice"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-s);">S *(Insane)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E1, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A supportive DPS who blasts enemies for high damage while boosting your Tentacle DMG and Tranquil Sea shields.

Her exalt takes time to set up, but deals huge AOE damage once prepared. With E3 and her wheel, it can one-shot endgame bosses.

Needs her posse, Reload! skill levels, and soulforge levels. She likes defensive teammates that can stall while she's ramping up.
</div>
</div>
</div>

## Caro

### Agrippa {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Alert Stalling Poison Tank
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Alert &middot;
    Embryo &middot;
    Poison &middot;
    Shields
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Agrippa"](/images/awakeners/caro/agrippa.png "Agrippa"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">*Support:* Any · *DPS:* E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Agrippa's exalt permanently stacks alert, boosting teamwide shields more and more over time. This makes her the ideal support for [Castor](#castor) stall teams that plan to survive forever.

She can also generate a lot of embryo and trigger poison for poison teams.

At high investment, Colorless Spiral applies a lot of poison with critical hits, making Agrippa herself usable as a poison DPS.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build (Support)</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build (Poison DPS)</div>
<div class="hagrid grid-1/1/1/1" markdown>

### Aigis {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Damage Multiplying Extra Turn Queen
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Stun &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    Keyflare &middot;
    Embryo &middot;
    Final DMG
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Aigis"](/images/awakeners/caro/aigis.png "Aigis"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-s);">S *(Insane)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">Any, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Aigis's unique petrify ability effectively gives you an extra turn in every fight.

She's also the best vulnerable applier in the game, and an excellent keyflare and embryo generator, and her OE grants a +25% Final DMG bonus.

Aigis is a great support for any team, but she pairs especially well with glass cannon DPS who need a turn of breathing room to set up.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>

### Doresain {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Terror of Low-HP Enemies
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Execute Low-HP Enemies &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    STR &middot;
    Heals &middot;
    Pierce DMG
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Doresain"](/images/awakeners/caro/doresain.png "Doresain"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b-plus);">B+ *(Good Early)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">Any</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A burst DPS who snowballs with kills. He excels at executing enemies that are low on health. He can also generate a lot of STR, apply vulnerable, and heal.

Doresain is strong at low levels but falls off at endgame, especially against bosses with full HP bars and no minions for him to snack on. He works best with STR buffs and another damage dealer that can set up kills for him.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Faint {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Hard-to-Kill Death Resistance Tank
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Death Res. &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    Heals &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    Counter &middot;
    STR Down
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Faint"](/images/awakeners/caro/faint.png "Faint"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">Any, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Faint's exalt can stack tons of death resistance, buying multiple turns where you can survive any hit no matter how high the damage. This makes her a top-tier endgame support, as the more difficult a fight is, the better she is compared to other defensive characters.

Faint is often paired with [GDoll](#gdoll) for boss fights, but fits in any team that needs to live just a bit longer.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build</div>

  </figure>

    [![Burial Ground's Sighs](/images/covenants/burial-grounds-sighs.png "Burial Ground's Sighs"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#burial-grounds-sighs)
  </figure>
  <div></div>
</div>
<div class="caption text-center" markdown="span">[Burial Ground's Sighs](/handbook/team#burial-grounds-sighs)</div>
</section>

    </figure>

    </figure>
  </div>

    </figure>
  </div>
</div>
</section>

### Helot {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Strike Buff Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Strike DMG Multiplier &middot;
    Strikes &middot;
    Dispel Weakness
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Helot"](/images/awakeners/caro/helot.png "Helot"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">*Support:* Any · *DPS:* E1, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Helot's exalt draws two strikes from your deck and multiplies all damage from strikes for that turn. This makes her a fantastic support for strike-based DPS like [Mouchette](#mouchette) and [GHelot](#ghelot).

Helot can also be built as a DPS that focuses on setting up huge Shattering Strikes. However, she needs a lot of setup that clogs your hand with bad cards, and has trouble killing normal enemies fast.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### GHelot {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Devastating Bleed Combo DPS
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Bleed &middot;
    Strikes &middot;
    Heals &middot;
    Remove Enemy Shields
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["GHelot"](/images/awakeners/caro/ghelot.png "GHelot"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c-plus);">C+ *(Niche)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Playing Crimson Shackles 3 times gives you Bloodthirsty Flail, a powerful card with prepare and retain. By copying this card over and over with the Lone Seed posse and [Thais](#thais), GHelot can set up a full hand of Flails and use her exalt to pull off one-shot combo turns.

Needs E3 and The Lone Seed for consistency. She works best with [Aigis](#aigis) or other teammates who can buy time while she's setting up.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build</div>

### Leigh {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Healer for Living Dangerously
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Heals &middot;
    Embryo &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    STR &middot;
    Pierce DMG &middot;
    Dispel Vulnerable
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Leigh"](/images/awakeners/caro/leigh.png "Leigh"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">Any, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A dedicated healer who heals for a ton when you're low on HP. This makes her a good partner for characters that stay under a HP threshold like [Uvhash](#uvhash) and [Sorel](#sorel).

Leigh makes a lot of embryo when roused, and her OE is a good source of STR too. Unlike [Faint](#faint), she doesn't have diminishing returns in long explorations, so you can use her to carry your squishy DPS through fight after fight.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build</div>

### Pickman {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Temporary Buff Stacking Sub DPS
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Discover &middot;
    STR Steal &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Aliemus &middot;
    Embryo &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span>
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Pickman"](/images/awakeners/caro/pickman.png "Pickman"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E2, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A support and secondary DPS who can access many effects with his painted orisons and relics.

By Discovering a lot, Pickman can make a pile of relics and spam Chromaphage for AOE damage and temporary STR. This gives a huge one-turn damage boost to your main DPS.

Works best with a main DPS that relies on their exalt and doesn't need arithmetica. The posse Voracious Resolve is highly recommended.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Salvador {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Immortal Crimson Furnace Tank
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Shields &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Crimson Furnace &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    Barrier
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Salvador"](/images/awakeners/caro/salvador.png "Salvador"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">*Support:* Any · *DPS:* E2, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A tough defensive support who generates Crimson Furnace and makes huge shields with End of Suffering. He also has access to both weakness and vulnerable.

If you copy End of Suffering over and over with the Lone Seed posse and [Thais](#thais), Salvador can be used as a slow, grindy, unkillable carry.

Works best with high-CON teammates, as your Crimson Furnace scales with your max HP.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Sorel {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Greedy Multihit Exalt DPS
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Multihit &middot;
    Heals &middot;
    Temp. STR &middot;
    Embryo &middot;
    Crit Rate
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Sorel"](/images/awakeners/caro/sorel.png "Sorel"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">Any, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A DPS who is completely reliant on other characters to feed her embryos, STR, and damage buffs. While she's weak at low investment, her exalt deals serious damage when enabled by a team of dedicated supports.

Usually seen with [Pickman](#pickman), as he builds STR for her and massively buffs her exalt. She also works well in Aequor/Caro as she triggers lots of tentacle hits in Raging Waves stance.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Thais {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Overpowered Support Goddess of Caro
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Embryo &middot;
    Card Copy &middot;
    Keyflare &middot;
    Aliemus &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    STR
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Thais"](/images/awakeners/caro/thais.png "Thais"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-s);">S *(Insane)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E1, E2, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
When a gacha company runs low on money, they release a character like Thais.

Thais is the best embryo maker, an excellent keyflare and aliemus generator, a card copying machine, and an overall ridiculous support who does everything your DPS could possibly want.

At E2 she is the best support for almost every team. The only reason she isn't in every "Works Well With" section is it would be redundant.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build (Keyflare Support)</div>
<div class="hagrid grid-1/1/1/1" markdown>
  <div></div>
  <figure class="center" markdown="span">
    [![Life Drain](/images/covenants/life-drain--icon.png "Life Drain"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#life-drain)
  </figure>
  <figure class="center" markdown="span">
    [![Life Drain](/images/covenants/life-drain.png "Life Drain"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#life-drain)
  </figure>
  <div></div>
</div>
<div class="caption text-center" markdown="span">[Life Drain](/handbook/team#life-drain)</div>
</section>

<section class="section" markdown>
<div class="hagrid grid-mobile-1/1 grid-desktop-1/1/1" markdown>
  <div class="heading text-center desktop">Example Build (Keyflare Support)</div>
  <div class="heading text-center">Early Game Wheels</div>
  <div class="heading text-center">Astral Reign Wheels</div>
</div>
<div class="hagrid grid-mobile-1/1 grid-desktop-1/1/1" markdown>
  <div class="desktop center" markdown>
  <div class="hagrid grid-1/1" markdown="span">
    <figure class="center">

### Uvhash {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Unsealable Self-Harming Berserker
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Immune to Seal &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Scaling &middot;
    Multihit &middot;
    STR
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Uvhash"](/images/awakeners/caro/uvhash.png "Uvhash"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *at OE*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A damage dealer who needs to stay under 25% HP to reach his full potential. Unfortunately, his full potential isn't terribly impressive compared to other options.

Uvhash's rouse makes him immune to being sealed. This gives him a niche, as he can ignore mechanics that other DPS might struggle with.

OE makes him a decent if fragile endgame DPS.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Xu {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Defensive Support & Poison Trigger Queen
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Poison &middot;
    Unique Debuff &middot;
    STR Down &middot;
    Arith. &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Embryo &middot;
    HP % Damage
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Xu"](/images/awakeners/caro/xu.png "Xu"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b-plus);">B+ *(Good Early)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E2, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A flexible support with good abilities and powerful debuffs. Her high CON boosts your max HP and thus poison cap in [Astral Reign](/handbook/storylines#astral-reign-arc-2).

Her exalt and Bonesick Longing are the biggest poison triggers in the game. This makes her an amazing secondary DPS in poison teams, often outdamaging the actual poison applier.

Can solo carry at low levels, but works best with a dedicated poison applier on the team.
</div>
</div>
</div>

## Propagation: Caro

### Saya {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Corrosion Nuker & Combo Setup Artist
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Corrosion &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Discard &middot;
    Card Draw &middot;
    Card Copy &middot;
    Aliemus &middot;
    Arith. &middot;
    Shield
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Saya"](/images/awakeners/caro/saya.png "Saya"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">F *(???)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-s);">S *(Insane)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E1</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Viscera Blossoms applies an absurd amount of corrosion, multiplying your damage by 4x and enabling even [bottom-tier DPS](/handbook/tier-list) to clear.

Saya can also funnel aliemus to her teammates, or seed your deck with 0-cost copies of their cards, setting up crazy plays for future turns.

She discards cards and messes with your hand, so she works best with teammates that don't need specific cards to function.
</div>
</div>
</div>

## Ultra

### Casiah {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Deck-Cycling Card Trick Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Card Draw &middot;
    Card Copy &middot;
    Discard Symptoms &middot;
    Multihit &middot;
    Temp. STR &middot;
    Strikes
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Casiah"](/images/awakeners/ultra/casiah.png "Casiah"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">Any</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A dedicated card draw support who fills your hand, replays cards from Ultra Space, and sets up multi-card combo turns for your DPS.

Often run in Aftershock-focused teams to draw and discard full hands of cards. In [Astral Reign](/handbook/storylines#astral-reign-arc-2) stages, Poof! can trigger Aftershock as well.

Her Astral Reign image relic makes her exalt inflict permanent STR down, enabling silly stall strategies against bosses that don't scale.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Castor {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Corrosive Shield Stall Tank
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Shields &middot;
    Corrosion &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    Card Draw
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Castor"](/images/awakeners/ultra/castor.png "Castor"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b-plus);">B+ *(Good Early)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">*Support:* Any, OE · *DPS:* E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A shielder who hoards Onyx Plumes in hand to accumulate shields at the end of each turn.

By himself, he's a great defensive support for any team. When paired with teammates that buff shields like [Agrippa](#agrippa) and [Erica](#erica), he can stall the hardest bosses forever.

Castor can deal solid damage by tossing Plumes to inflict corrosion stacks, but you need another source of damage to trigger the corrosion.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>

### Clementine {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Universal Buffing Keyflare Support-Carry
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Unique Debuffs &middot;
    Keyflare &middot;
    STR &middot;
    Heals &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Multihit
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Clementine"](/images/awakeners/ultra/clementine.png "Clementine"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-s);">S *(Insane)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">*Support:* Any, OE · *DPS:* E2</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Clementine is the best keyflare generator and the best STR stacking support in the game. The unique debuffs from her exalt are multiplicative with weakness, vulnerable, and Final DMG.

She is also an excellent healer when roused, and at E2, her exalt hits so hard that she can end mob fights by herself.

She works best with DPS that rely on STR, but improves basically any team by being on it.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build (Keyflare Support)</div>
<div class="hagrid grid-1/1/1/1" markdown>
  <div></div>
  <figure class="center" markdown="span">
    [![Life Drain](/images/covenants/life-drain--icon.png "Life Drain"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#life-drain)
  </figure>
  <figure class="center" markdown="span">
    [![Life Drain](/images/covenants/life-drain.png "Life Drain"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#life-drain)
  </figure>
  <div></div>
</div>
<div class="caption text-center" markdown="span">[Life Drain](/handbook/team#life-drain)</div>
</section>

### Daffodil {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Counter & Poison Combo Witch
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Temp. Counter &middot;
    Poison &middot;
    Card Draw &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Crit Rate
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Daffodil"](/images/awakeners/ultra/daffodil.png "Daffodil"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E2, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A burst DPS with a lot of small utility bonuses on her cards. At low levels, Skull Reaver scales with last hits and deals a lot of damage.

At endgame Daffodil is used for her Thousand Mirages, which make tons of temporary counter or poison. This enables high-damage combo turns with [Arachne](#arachne), [Nautila](#nautila), etc.

Her OE puts three Mirages in hand, enabling silly burst damage with high investment.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Erica {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Alert Stalling Keyflare Bot
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Temp. Alert &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    Keyflare &middot;
    Dispel Fragile/Weakness
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Erica"](/images/awakeners/ultra/erica.png "Erica"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E1, E3</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A free keyflare support with a strong exalt that inflicts weakness and vulnerable.

Once roused, she generates temporary alert each time she makes a shield. With Function Overload, she can make a huge shield and a huge one-turn buff to all your shielding.

Usually seen in stall teams with [Castor](#castor) because each Onyx Plume benefits individually from alert, allowing [Castor](#castor) to stack giant shields.
</div>
</div>
</div>
