### Horla {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Universal Multiplier Aura Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Moods &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-vulnerable)">Vulnerable</span> &middot;
    Aliemus &middot;
    Crit Rate &middot;
    Crit DMG &middot;
    Heals
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Horla"](/images/awakeners/ultra/horla.png "Horla"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">F *(???)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-s);">S *(Insane)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E1, E2</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A support who passively multiplies your damage, defense, aliemus generation, or STR, scaling with her death resistance.

If a character had just one of Horla's moods, they would be a powerful support character. Horla's ability to switch on the fly makes her close to an auto-include in any team.

E1 is recommended, as it makes her one of the best debuff appliers and easy to slot anywhere.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section" markdown>
<div class="hagrid grid-mobile-1/2 grid-desktop-1/4 desktop" markdown>

  <div class="heading center">(Any)</div>
  <div class="grid-mobile-1/1 grid-desktop-1/1/1/1" markdown>
  <figure markdown="span">
  [![Pollux](/images/awakeners/ultra/pollux--mini.png "Pollux"){loading=lazy}](#pollux) <figcaption>[Pollux](#pollux)</figcaption>
  </figure>
  <figure markdown="span">
  [![GHelot](/images/awakeners/caro/ghelot--mini.png "GHelot"){loading=lazy}](#ghelot) <figcaption>[GHelot](#ghelot)</figcaption>
  </figure>

  [![Kathigu-Ra](/images/awakeners/chaos/kathigu-ra--mini.png "Kathigu-Ra"){loading=lazy}](#kathigu-ra) <figcaption>[Kathigu-Ra](#kathigu-ra)</figcaption>
  </figure>
  <figure markdown="span">
  ![](/images/emojis/aigis-questioning.png){loading=lazy} <figcaption>(Anyone)</figcaption>
  </figure>
</div>
</section>

### Jenkin {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Multihit Crit Buff Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Crit DMG &middot;
    Crit Rate &middot;
    Multihit &middot;
    AOE
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Jenkin"](/images/awakeners/ultra/jenkin.png "Jenkin"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">*Support:* Any · *DPS:* E1, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
Jenkin's exalt and rouse make buckets of Crit DMG and Crit Rate, making her a strong damage buffer for any damage dealer that can crit. She also does a lot of AOE hits which can be used for popping barriers or tanking Chains of Resentment.

Jenkin can work as a main DPS herself, but needs high levels or STR buffs to do enough damage against endgame bosses.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Liz {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    High-Maintenance Poison DPS
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Poison &middot;
    Multihit &middot;
    Discard &middot;
    Card Draw &middot;
    Pierce DMG
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Liz"](/images/awakeners/ultra/liz.png "Liz"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">F *(???)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E1, E2, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A finicky but rewarding poison applier. If you babysit Liz enough to set up her exalt, she applies massive amounts of poison with Deadly Flames and becomes the best sustained damage dealer on the standard banner.

Hard to use early on, but gets much better with teammates that give her defense, aliemus, and STR. Also prefers her posse, E1 or better, and a hand size wheel carried by one of her supports.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>

### Pollux {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Scaling Glass Cannon Combo DPS
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Bleed &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Card Draw &middot;
    Shields
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Pollux"](/images/awakeners/ultra/pollux.png "Pollux"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-a);">A *(Great)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A burst DPS who revolves around refreshing and abusing the Atonement by Pain buff, which boosts the first card he plays each turn.

Atonement by Pain gets stronger after every fight, making Pollux incredible in long explorations. However, he needs setup and works best with teammates that can buy time.

Needs E1 for consistency and E3 for high damage. OE makes him one of the top DPS.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Tinct {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Arithmetica and Crit Buff Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Arith. &middot;
    Crit Rate &middot;
    Crit DMG &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    Dispel Fragile/Weakness/Vulnerable
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Tinct"](/images/awakeners/ultra/tinct.png "Tinct"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E2, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
In addition to giving big crit buffs, Tinct discounts up to 5 arithmetica with every exalt, making her a perfect teammate for DPS that retain full hands of cards for combo turns.

Tinct dispels many debuffs and can even access weakness and vulnerable from her rouse (though not consistently).

At E2, her defense card becomes quite good, making her a usable shielder for Ultra teams.
</div>
</div>
</div>

### Wanda {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    STR Draining Counter Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Unique Debuff &middot;
    STR Down &middot;
    Counter &middot;
    Multihit
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Wanda"](/images/awakeners/ultra/wanda.png "Wanda"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c);">C *(Usable)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-c-plus);">C+ *(Niche)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E2, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A defensive support who inflicts a lot of STR down and forces enemies to attack in multiple small hits instead of one big hit.

While Wanda is strong at low levels, she needs high investment to keep up with enemy damage later on. At endgame, she's only good in specific stages that favor her.

Technically usable as a damage dealer, but works best with counter relics or a real DPS.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>

### Winkle {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Aliemus & Defensive Utility Support
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Aliemus &middot;
    <span style="color: var(--md-effect-weakness)">Weakness</span> &middot;
    Keyflare &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    Discard &middot;
    Remove Barrier &middot;
    Dispel Fragile
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Winkle"](/images/awakeners/ultra/winkle.png "Winkle"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading">D *(Meme)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b);">B *(Decent)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E3, OE</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A solid aliemus battery with a variety of defensive tools. While not the best at anything, she's a low-cost, well-rounded filler option for Ultra teams.

At E3, her exalt lets a teammate exalt twice in one turn. This is useful for characters who deal damage with their exalt, or who need to use their exalt over and over to work.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build</div>
<div class="hagrid grid-1/1/1/1" markdown>

  </figure>
  <figure class="center" markdown="span">
    [![Burial Ground's Sighs](/images/covenants/burial-grounds-sighs.png "Burial Ground's Sighs"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#burial-grounds-sighs)
  </figure>
  <figure class="center" markdown="span">
    [![Deus Ex Machina](/images/covenants/deus-ex-machina--icon.png "Deus Ex Machina"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#deus-ex-machina)
  </figure>
  <figure class="center" markdown="span">
    [![Deus Ex Machina](/images/covenants/deus-ex-machina.png "Deus Ex Machina"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#deus-ex-machina)
  </figure>
</div>
<div class="caption text-center" markdown="span">(Any support)</div>
</section>

      [![Burial Ground's Sighs](/images/covenants/burial-grounds-sighs--icon.png "Burial Ground's Sighs"){loading=lazy}](/handbook/team#burial-grounds-sighs)
    </figure>
    <figure class="center">

## Singularity: Ultra

### Arachne {.tier .text-center}

<div class="text-center" markdown style="margin-bottom: 24px;">
  <p class="heading" markdown="span" style="margin: 0;">
    Damage Amplifier, Harbinger of Doom
  </p>
  <p class="caption" markdown="span">
    Temp. Prism &middot;
    DMG Amp. &middot;
    Card Copy &middot;
    AOE &middot;
    Shields &middot;
    Dispel Stagnation
  </p>
</div>

<div class="flex-desktop" markdown>
<div markdown="span" style="flex-shrink: 0;">
  !["Arachne"](/images/awakeners/ultra/arachne.png "Arachne"){width="168" loading=lazy}
</div>
<div markdown>
<div class="grid cards grid-cards-tiers text-center" markdown>
  - <span class="caption">DPS Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-b-plus);">B+ *(Good Early)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Support Rank</span>

    <span class="heading" style="color: var(--md-tier-s);">S *(Insane)*</span>

  - <span class="caption">Stopping Points</span>

    <span class="heading">E0, E2, E3</span>
</div>
<div markdown>
A complex but powerful support. Her rouse and pursuit multiply the effectiveness of your team's command cards. She also brings good shields and huge [DMG amplification](/handbook/team#dmg-amplification-base-dmg) buffs.

Arachne's Final Verdict outdamages many DPS, while also ignoring shields and invulnerability, trivializing many boss mechanics.

She works best supporting a DPS that has good cards, but hits hard enough to solo many fights.
</div>
</div>
</div>

<section class="section mobile" markdown>
<div class="heading text-center">Example Build</div>
